	#Development only changes the de_jure territory. So no need to add dates for titles that no longer exist ie Lotharingia which is split into Upper/Lower Lorraine. Numbers are pretty arbitary and I'm not going to look up whether the Duchy of Blois was more 'developed' than the Duchy of Valois so their 1100 number will be the same just like it is in 1066. 
	#
	#   - Areas will lose development where needed. For example Constantinople during 1204 or parts of the Middle East due to Mongol Conquests such as Baghdad or Khwarazm.
	#	- Individual counties/duchies may be higher than the Kingdoms overall setting. Generally speaking this means major cities and capitals
	#
